<review>I recently had to make the hard decision to let one of my babies go to the rainbow bridge, after battling years of epilepsy. She was allergic to any medication that would control her seizures, so we opted to give her CBd and let her live as long as she could with quality. That being said, my vet met with me on her day off to look at her and to give me advice, and after gave me her personal number to call or text any concerns or questions I may have had. Almost two years later I had to have Gigi put down, it was a rough time, but the staff were so caring and helpful. The vet examined her and let me know I was making the right decision. There were tears In the eyes of the staff as they spoke with me and comforted me, that meant a lot and showed me that they care. A couple of days later I received a beautiful card in the mail letting me know how sorry they were for my loss, enclosed was the rainbow bridge poem. I will forever take my pets to a place where they care not only for the animals with compassion and love, they care for the person as well. I highly recommend this vet clinic.<//review><UserId.>111953371150620092498< /UserId.></record>

<Text>I will never go back here. I refrain from giving them one star because I hold myself partly responsible. I should have not blinded trusted this vet. I should have asked more questions, etc. My healthy young cat got an infection. The vet gave him Convenia. He got better but developed a heart murmur, which was diagnosed the morning of his neuter a week later. We were given the option of taking him to Fresno for a heart exam or to go thru w/ the neuter. We went through with the neuter because we thought it could have been from stress. I should have demanded blood work be done. In fact, looking back, all of my previous vets required blood work with any anesthesia. This might have discovered that he was anemic. I suspect from the Convenia. There is documentation online that this drug can cause this. I have been in contact with people whose pets died from anemia from this drug. The surgery required a second injection of this drug. I did questioned it but this vet assured us it would be fine. My cat died 5 days later from severe anemia. I spent over 2K on him and could not afford an autopsy. Plus, I was too distraught to even consider it at the time. Please question this vet or any vet. Research the drugs they give your babies. I am devastated. I wish this vet would have immediately considered other reasons for the murmur since it was undetected in 2 recent visits before doing the surgery. My cat might still be alive.<//Text><Gmap_id>0x809526229111d7d9:0x53f9d879e28517b9<//Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

<UserId.>115877894041291946702</UserId.>< user_name>
Josiah Head</user_name>
<time>1505445356261</time>< rate>
5<//rate>
< review>
*UPDATE for new business name*

Formerly Gents Barbershop of West Sacramento Hye Cuts Barbershop is a brand revitalization by the owner Mike, that brings to you a mixture of his Armenian heritage in the name 'Hye'. Along with his love of keeping patrons crispy, with a nice clean cut and or shave.

Tucked away within the plaza, this barbershop is surrounded by a mixture of businesses. But it's bustling with people outside. As you walk up to the fron entrance you'll notice the logo on the front of the door and you can't see inside as all of the windows is tinted. Once inside you'll notice the tint helps to cut down on the bright light from outside and to minimize heat on warmer days. But it makes for a nice feel inside.

When you walk in you're greeted by a nice bachelor pad type of vibe. Brick colored walls, brown hardwood floor, nice lighting, black leather couches and barber chairs make the shops atmosphere. And you're greeted by the barber's which is nice, as some shops you walk into act like you're not there; even if you're gonna be cut by them. As soon as my Mike (the owner) sees me, he'll come over and say hi, and greet my girlfriend and our boys if they're there with me.

Mike and the other barbers are always hooking their clients up with clean haircuts that show an attention to detail. With my cuts Mike always goes the extra mile with my hair and beard, and will will occasionally ask if I want a little bit of eyebrow clean up with the straight razor. That's one thing I like about going to Hye Cuts, the hot towel and straight razor treatment is the icing on the cake for a fresh haircut. And a lot of places just don't give you that treatment!

Overall: If you're in the area looking for a nice shop, that will give you a clean cut with a good internal environment. Then definitely check out this place!</review>

This is my go to destination after a trail run or a motorcycle ride, when I want good coffee or to show a friend how cool I am for knowing about this cool trendy place. I always get a wrap and tater tots with French fry sauce and coffee. I love these things so much, I can't bring myself to order something new/different. I would suggest trying the brownie because it is the chocolatey-est most gorgeous thing ever. There are signs posted indicating that these white front-load washers are not designed for materials that absorb a lot of water; such as jeans, sweatshirts, sweaters, towels, jackets, pillows, blankets, sleeping bags, etc.  These items become heavy when wet & the white front-load washers are not designed to spin the heavier loads.  That is why your laundry came out wet, why the machine made noises & why it took longer to do your wash.  We do have silver machines designed to handle these heavier loads & you would have been very happy with the results if you had used the silver machines (same price). <userid>117521536790262405271< /userid><time>1556171212102<//time>< text>
By far the best Retro Arcade I have been to. It is easy to kill an hour or two playing the games. I myself can spend an hour or two on $5-10 which is incredibly cheap for this day and age. Besides classics we know they even have a couple rhythum games imported from Japan still running on their native software. What is nice is you can even book private parties for $225 for 4 hours. Not too shabby. It really is a diamond in the rough. One of the photos I added is of my high Score. If you visit soon enough you will see that ATA holds that high score and is tops of that one. Even if you do not like coin arcade games you can rent current gen consoles for use in the back room for game tournaments. There is nothing bad I can say the people working there are wonderful.<//text>

<Review>Stopped in for a cup of espresso on the way to LAX and I'm glad I did, because I needed a shot of ceffeine, stat! We got a latte, and ordered an Iced Lavender latte with Oatmilk.

They messed up the iced latte and gave us a matcha instead, they remade our drink and told us to keep the matcha and it turns out that was the favorite.

Try the Iced Lavender Matcha with Oatmilk, the matcha was creamy and flavorful, the lavender was subtle and sweet and the Oatmilk was deep and rich. The flavors complimented each other like dancers choreographed to a symphony.

The place seemed like a cool place to sit down and do some work although we only had a few moments to talk over in the patio. Not too busy, would definitely check out this place!<//Review>< Rate>

<userid>104971071022870592232< /userid>< Name>

< review>
I'm not a reviewer that is stingy with his stars, nor do I throw them carelessly and irresponsibly at places to skew the honest opinions of customers.. When I award someone five stars, they've earned them. They've met the expectations of an establishment that does exactly what they're supposed to, exactly what they promise to, and exactly what I'll return to.

Blue Butterfly Coffee Co. was out of the way for my plans for the day, but I needed a spot to sit and do some work. When I arrived, I was sad to not see any open seats where I could set up camp and get my work done, so I just ordered a cortado and French toast and hopped up to the beautiful wooden bar.

I didn't watch them make my drink, too busy trying to watch everything else in this bustling shop. The super quiet Malkhonig conical grinder spat out its dose. Each dose is carefully spun with a grounds distributor, and then tamped with a mechanical tamp. They've spared no expense to get all the variables of espresso in line.. I couldn't discern what milk was used, but when I received my drink I didn't care much...this was one of the top three cortados I've had anywhere.. The only improvement would be to give the coffee in the glass a quick stir before topping with milk...

The French toast came sprinkled with powered sugar and a side of real, warm maple syrup.. Ahh, real maple syrup... Some of the best breakfast establishments I've been to still refuse to offer this natural condiment with their cakes and toasts, but this coffee shop gives more than I'd ever need. Such a relief..

Great French toast. Great cortado.. I think I'll have some tea next.</review>

<Name>Christopher Lai< /Name><Date>1550398895376</Date><Rating>4< /Rating>< text>
I came to Blue Butterfly during my lunch break and it was decently busy. I was looking for a local coffee shop with pastries and Blue Butterfly fit the bill.

I got an medium iced latte which was good, but too milky for my taste. I like really tasting the coffee so the next time I come, I'd either add a shot to my drink or get something without milk. I also got an almond croissant which was super good and buttery when heated up. I want to try the chocolate croissant next time :)

They also have a good amount of whole beans for sale in bags. The roast dates are printed and from what I could tell, nothing was more than 1-2 weeks old. Fresh! If only there was more coffee in my latte!! If I liked the coffee, I definitely would have bought a bag of beans for home.< /text>

Blue Butterfly Coffee Co. fulfills my coffee snobbery with some excellent coffee. Their cold brew is delicious, they said it is typically a Mexican and Guatemalan blend, it starts off with a cedar and orange flavor, then upon the second sip the tangy, coffee fruit flavours come out. Delicious! I also had their Kenyan one day it they brew a good cup of coffee. I usually use a 1/16 ratio and their coffee is pretty darn close if not the same ratio. They also had a good Kenyan when I was there, served at a perfect temperature. They also have bags of beans for purchase if you do your own grinding and coffee.<//Review>
